pattern 1/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=4 diamonds=4 branches=0 complete=true
110100000100100100000010000110010000010010100000000000000000000000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r4c5, [r1c2=r4c1], r4c2, r5c2} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—r4c2).
      → color(r4c5) = color(r5c2). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c1], r2c4, r3c5} (spine [r1c4=r2c1]—r2c4).
      → color(r2c7) = color(r3c5). Identify.
  5.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r3c5], [r4c5=r5c2], r5c5, r5c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 3/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=7 diamonds=7 branches=0 complete=true
110100000100100100000000000110100000010000110000000100000000000000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c2} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c2). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r2c4} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r2c4). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {[r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r2c7} (spine [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c1=r4c4]) = color(r2c7). Identify.
  7.  Diamond {[r1c1=r2c7=r4c4], [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r5c2} (spine [r1c2=r2c4=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c1=r2c7=r4c4]) = color(r5c2). Identify.
  8.  K₄ on {[r1c1=r2c7=r4c4=r5c2], r5c7, r5c8, r6c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r4c7) = color(r7c2). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r3c5, [r1c4=r2c1], r2c4, r7c4} (spine [r1c4=r2c1]—r2c4).

  5.  K₄ on {[r3c5=r7c4], r3c7, [r4c7=r7c2], r7c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c2} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c2). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r7c4} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r7c4). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {[r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1=r7c4], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], r7c2} (spine [r1c2=r4c1=r7c4]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]).
      → color([r1c1=r4c4]) = color(r7c2). Identify.
  7.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2], [r1c1=r4c4=r7c2], [r1c2=r4c1=r7c4], r7c7} (spine [r1c1=r4c4=r7c2]—[r1c2=r4c1=r7c4]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1=r4c2]) = color(r7c7). Identify.
  8.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c2=r7c7], r3c5, r3c6, r3c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Branch on [r1c4=r2c1], r5c5:
      Case A: color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r5c5). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r5c5], r5c2} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r5c5]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r5c2). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r5c5], [r1c1=r5c2], [r1c2=r4c1], r6c3} (spine [r1c1=r5c2]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r5c5]) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r5c5=r6c3], r2c7, r5c7, r6c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color([r1c4=r2c1]) ≠ color(r5c5). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], r3c5, r5c5, r6c5} (spine r3c5—r5c5).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r6c5], r6c3} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r6c5]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r6c5], [r1c1=r6c3], [r1c2=r4c1], r5c2} (spine [r1c1=r6c3]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r6c5]) = color(r5c2). Identify.
        10.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r5c2=r6c5], r2c7, r5c7, r6c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 128/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=7 diamonds=7 branches=1 complete=true
110100000100000100000000000100100000010010100001010100000000000000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
  4.  Branch on r5c2, r6c5:
      Case A: color(r5c2) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], [r5c2=r6c5]} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color([r5c2=r6c5]). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r5c2=r6c5], r2c7, r5c7, r6c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r5c2) ≠ color(r6c5). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {r5c7, r5c2, r5c5, r6c5} (spine r5c2—r5c5).
            → color(r5c7) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {r5c5, r5c2, [r5c7=r6c5], r6c3} (spine r5c2—[r5c7=r6c5]).
            → color(r5c5) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], [r5c5=r6c3]} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color([r5c5=r6c3]). Identify.
        10.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r5c5=r6c3], r2c7, [r5c7=r6c5], r6c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

        9.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], [r5c5=r6c3]} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color([r5c5=r6c3]). Identify.
        10.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r5c5=r6c3], r2c7, [r5c7=r6c6], r6c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c5} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c5). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c5], r3c4} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c5]).
      → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r3c4). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {[r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r3c4=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c5], r3c5} (spine [r1c2=r3c4=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c5]).
      → color([r1c1=r4c4]) = color(r3c5). Identify.
  7.  Diamond {[r1c2=r3c4=r4c1], [r1c1=r3c5=r4c4], [r1c4=r2c1=r4c5], r9c5} (spine [r1c1=r3c5=r4c4]—[r1c4=r2c1=r4c5]).
      → color([r1c2=r3c4=r4c1]) = color(r9c5). Identify.
  8.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r3c4=r4c1=r9c5], r7c2, r8c2, r9c3}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r4c7) = color(r5c4). Identify.

  6.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1=r7c4], r7c2, r7c3, r8c2}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).

  3.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
  4.  Branch on r3c5, r7c2:
      Case A: color(r3c5) = color(r7c2). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], [r3c5=r7c2]} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).

        6.  K₄ on {[r1c1=r3c5=r4c4=r7c2], r3c6, r5c6, r7c6}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r3c5) ≠ color(r7c2). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {r5c5, r3c5, r7c5, r7c2} (spine r3c5—r7c5).
            → color(r5c5) = color(r7c2). Identify.

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).

      → color(r7c2) = color(r9c5). Identify.
  6.  K₄ on {[r7c2=r9c5], r7c7, r9c7, r9c8}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 215/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=7 diamonds=8 branches=1 complete=true
110100000100000000000000000100000100000000000000000000010000000001100100001100100
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Branch on r8c4, r9c3:
      Case A: color(r8c4) = color(r9c3). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r7c2, r8c3, [r8c4=r9c3], r8c7} (spine r8c3—[r8c4=r9c3]).
            → color(r7c2) = color(r8c7). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], r4c7, [r7c2=r8c7], r9c7} (spine r4c7—[r7c2=r8c7]).
            → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r9c7). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1=r9c7], [r1c4=r2c1], [r8c4=r9c3], r9c4}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r8c4) ≠ color(r9c3). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {r8c7, r8c3, r8c4, r9c3} (spine r8c3—r8c4).
            → color(r8c7) = color(r9c3). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {r7c2, r8c3, [r8c7=r9c3], r8c4} (spine r8c3—[r8c7=r9c3]).
            → color(r7c2) = color(r8c4). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], [r7c2=r8c4]} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
            → color(r1c1) = color([r7c2=r8c4]). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {[r1c2=r4c1], [r1c1=r7c2=r8c4], [r1c4=r2c1], r9c4} (spine [r1c1=r7c2=r8c4]—[r1c4=r2c1]).
            → color([r1c2=r4c1]) = color(r9c4). Identify.
        11.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c1=r9c4], r4c7, [r8c7=r9c3], r9c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

110100000100000000000100110100000110000000000000000000000100110000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Branch on [r1c4=r2c1], r3c7:
      Case A: color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r3c7). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r3c7], r4c7} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r4c7). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7], [r1c1=r4c7], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c8} (spine [r1c1=r4c7]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r3c7]) = color(r4c8). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7=r4c8], r7c4, r7c7, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color([r1c4=r2c1]) ≠ color(r3c7). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {r3c7, [r1c4=r2c1], r3c4, r7c4} (spine [r1c4=r2c1]—r3c4).
            → color(r3c7) = color(r7c4). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], r3c4, [r3c7=r7c4], r3c8} (spine r3c4—[r3c7=r7c4]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r3c8). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r3c8], r4c8} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r3c8]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r4c8). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c8], [r1c1=r4c8], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c7} (spine [r1c1=r4c8]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r3c8]) = color(r4c7). Identify.
        11.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c8=r4c7], [r3c7=r7c4], r7c7, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], r3c5, r3c6, r3c7} (spine r3c5—r3c6).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r3c7). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r3c7], r4c7} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7]).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r4c7). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7], [r1c1=r4c7], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c5} (spine [r1c1=r4c7]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1=r3c7]) = color(r4c5). Identify.
  6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7=r4c5], r7c4, r7c5, r8c4}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 249/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=6 diamonds=7 branches=1 complete=true
110100000100000000000010110100000110000000000000000000000100110000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c1], r4c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c1]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Branch on [r1c4=r2c1], r3c7:
      Case A: color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r3c7). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r3c7], r4c7} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r4c7). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7], [r1c1=r4c7], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c8} (spine [r1c1=r4c7]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r3c7]) = color(r4c8). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c7=r4c8], r7c4, r7c7, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color([r1c4=r2c1]) ≠ color(r3c7). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], r3c5, r3c7, r3c8} (spine r3c5—r3c7).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r3c8). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1=r3c8], r4c8} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1=r3c8]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r4c8). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c8], [r1c1=r4c8], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c7} (spine [r1c1=r4c8]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c1=r3c8]) = color(r4c7). Identify.
        10.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r3c8=r4c7], r7c4, r7c7, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r4c7, r5c7, r5c8, r5c4} (spine r5c7—r5c8).
      → color(r4c7) = color(r5c4). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c1], [r4c7=r5c4]} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c1]).

  5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], [r1c1=r4c7=r5c4], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c5} (spine [r1c1=r4c7=r5c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c5). Identify.
  6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c5], r7c4, r8c5, r9c5}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  5.  K₄ on {[r4c5=r8c7], r4c6, [r4c7=r7c5], r8c6}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  6.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r3c5=r4c8], r7c7, r8c8, r9c8}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c1], r4c4, r5c4, r4c5} (spine r4c4—r5c4).
      → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color(r4c5). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c1=r4c5], r2c5, r7c5} (spine [r1c4=r2c1=r4c5]—r2c5).
      → color(r2c7) = color(r7c5). Identify.
  4.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r7c5], r7c8, r8c7, r9c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r4c4, r8c7:
      Case A: color(r4c4) = color(r8c7). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c1], r2c7, [r4c4=r8c7]} (spine [r1c4=r2c1]—r2c7).
            → color(r2c5) = color([r4c4=r8c7]). Identify.
        4.  K₄ on {[r2c5=r4c4=r8c7], r7c4, r7c5, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r4c4) ≠ color(r8c7). Add edge.
        5.  Diamond {r4c5, r4c4, r4c7, r8c7} (spine r4c4—r4c7).
            → color(r4c5) = color(r8c7). Identify.

        7.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c5=r8c7], r7c4, r7c5, r7c8}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

            → color(r4c6) = color(r7c5). Identify.

            → color([r1c4=r2c1]) = color([r4c6=r7c5]). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c1=r4c6=r7c5], r2c7, [r4c7=r7c6], r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c1} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c1). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r2c7, r5c7, r6c7, r4c8} (spine r5c7—r6c7).
      → color(r2c7) = color(r4c8). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {[r2c7=r4c8], [r1c4=r2c1], r4c4, r7c4} (spine [r1c4=r2c1]—r4c4).
      → color([r2c7=r4c8]) = color(r7c4). Identify.
  4.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r4c8=r7c4], r7c9, r8c8, r9c8}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 424/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=6 diamonds=6 branches=1 complete=true
110100000001000000000000000100100100100100100001000000001000100000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r1c1, r4c1, r5c1, r6c3} (spine r4c1—r5c1).
      → color(r1c1) = color(r6c3). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r1c2, [r1c1=r6c3], [r1c4=r2c3], r7c3} (spine [r1c1=r6c3]—[r1c4=r2c3]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r7c3). Identify.
  4.  Branch on r4c1, r7c7:
      Case A: color(r4c1) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], [r1c1=r6c3], [r1c2=r7c3], [r4c1=r7c7]} (spine [r1c1=r6c3]—[r1c2=r7c3]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color([r4c1=r7c7]). Identify.
        6.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c3=r4c1=r7c7], r5c1, r5c4, r5c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r4c1) ≠ color(r7c7). Add edge.
        7.  Diamond {r4c4, r4c1, r4c7, r7c7} (spine r4c1—r4c7).
            → color(r4c4) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        8.  Diamond {[r1c1=r6c3], [r1c2=r7c3], [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c4=r7c7]} (spine [r1c2=r7c3]—[r1c4=r2c3]).
            → color([r1c1=r6c3]) = color([r4c4=r7c7]). Identify.
        9.  K₄ on {[r1c1=r4c4=r6c3=r7c7], r5c1, r5c4, r5c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r4c5, r4c1, r4c2, r6c3} (spine r4c1—r4c2).
      → color(r4c5) = color(r6c3). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c5=r6c3], r5c4} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r4c5=r6c3]).
      → color(r2c5) = color(r5c4). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {[r4c5=r6c3], [r1c4=r2c3], [r2c5=r5c4], r7c4} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r2c5=r5c4]).
      → color([r4c5=r6c3]) = color(r7c4). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], [r2c5=r5c4], [r4c5=r6c3=r7c4], r7c5} (spine [r2c5=r5c4]—[r4c5=r6c3=r7c4]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r7c5). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3=r7c5], r7c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3=r7c5]).
      → color(r1c2) = color(r7c1). Identify.
  7.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r7c1], r4c1, r4c2, [r4c5=r6c3=r7c4]}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r1c2, r4c1:
      Case A: color(r1c2) = color(r4c1). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], r7c1} (spine r1c1—[r1c2=r4c1]).
            → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r7c1). Identify.
        4.  Diamond {r1c1, [r1c2=r4c1], [r1c4=r2c3=r7c1], r4c4} (spine [r1c2=r4c1]—[r1c4=r2c3=r7c1]).
            → color(r1c1) = color(r4c4). Identify.
        5.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3=r7c1], [r1c1=r4c4], [r1c2=r4c1], r4c7} (spine [r1c1=r4c4]—[r1c2=r4c1]).

        11.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c3=r4c1=r8c2], r2c7, r4c7, r8c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  4.  Diamond {r1c1, r1c2, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c4=r5c2]} (spine r1c2—[r1c4=r2c3]).
      → color(r1c1) = color([r4c4=r5c2]). Identify.

Proof of non-3-colorability:

      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r1c1, r7c7:
      Case A: color(r1c1) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r1c2, [r1c1=r7c7], [r1c4=r2c3], r2c7} (spine [r1c1=r7c7]—[r1c4=r2c3]).

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  3.  Diamond {r5c2, r4c1, [r6c3=r7c4], r7c1} (spine r4c1—[r6c3=r7c4]).
      → color(r5c2) = color(r7c1). Identify.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r5c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r5c3, r8c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r5c3).

      → color(r4c4) = color(r5c3). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r4c1, [r4c4=r5c3], r4c7, r5c7} (spine [r4c4=r5c3]—r4c7).

  6.  K₄ on {[r4c1=r5c7], [r4c7=r5c4=r8c3], r7c1, r7c7}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r1c1) = color(r5c4). Identify.

      → color([r1c2=r7c1=r8c4]) = color(r4c5). Identify.
  7.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r4c5=r7c1=r8c4], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c1], r4c3, r9c3}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r4c7) = color(r7c5). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r4c5, [r2c7=r3c5], [r4c7=r7c5], r7c7} (spine [r2c7=r3c5]—[r4c7=r7c5]).
      → color(r4c5) = color(r7c7). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r2c7=r3c5], [r4c5=r7c7], [r4c7=r7c5], r4c1} (spine [r4c5=r7c7]—[r4c7=r7c5]).
      → color([r2c7=r3c5]) = color(r4c1). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {r1c2, r1c1, [r1c4=r2c3], [r2c7=r3c5=r4c1]} (spine r1c1—[r1c4=r2c3]).
      → color(r1c2) = color([r2c7=r3c5=r4c1]). Identify.
  7.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r2c7=r3c5=r4c1], [r4c5=r7c7], [r4c7=r7c5], r7c2}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r4c5, r5c3:
      Case A: color(r4c5) = color(r5c3). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r3c6, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, [r4c5=r5c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).

        5.  Diamond {r4c6, r4c1, r4c5, r5c3} (spine r4c1—r4c5).
            → color(r4c6) = color(r5c3). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r2c5, [r1c4=r2c3], r3c6, [r4c6=r5c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r3c6).

        7.  K₄ on {[r2c5=r4c6=r5c3], r7c3, r7c5, r7c6}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      → color(r2c7) = color(r3c5). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r4c7, [r2c7=r3c5], r4c5, r7c5} (spine [r2c7=r3c5]—r4c5).
      → color(r4c7) = color(r7c5). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r4c5, [r2c7=r3c5], [r4c7=r7c5], r8c7} (spine [r2c7=r3c5]—[r4c7=r7c5]).
      → color(r4c5) = color(r8c7). Identify.
  5.  K₄ on {[r4c5=r8c7], [r4c7=r7c5], r4c8, r7c8}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 658/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=5 diamonds=5 branches=1 complete=true
110100000001010000000100100001010100001010100000000000000000000000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r4c3, r5c5:
      Case A: color(r4c3) = color(r5c5). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, [r4c3=r5c5]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
            → color(r3c4) = color([r4c3=r5c5]). Identify.
        4.  K₄ on {[r3c4=r4c3=r5c5], r3c7, r4c7, r5c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r4c3) ≠ color(r5c5). Add edge.
        5.  Diamond {r4c7, r4c3, r4c5, r5c5} (spine r4c3—r4c5).
            → color(r4c7) = color(r5c5). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r4c5, r4c3, [r4c7=r5c5], r5c3} (spine r4c3—[r4c7=r5c5]).
            → color(r4c5) = color(r5c3). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, [r4c5=r5c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
            → color(r3c4) = color([r4c5=r5c3]). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r3c4=r4c5=r5c3], r3c7, [r4c7=r5c5], r5c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

        3.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, [r4c3=r7c5]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
            → color(r3c4) = color([r4c3=r7c5]). Identify.
        4.  K₄ on {[r3c4=r4c3=r7c5], r3c7, r4c7, r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r4c3) ≠ color(r7c5). Add edge.
        5.  Diamond {r4c7, r4c3, r4c5, r7c5} (spine r4c3—r4c5).
            → color(r4c7) = color(r7c5). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r4c5, r4c3, [r4c7=r7c5], r7c3} (spine r4c3—[r4c7=r7c5]).
            → color(r4c5) = color(r7c3). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c5, [r4c5=r7c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c5).
            → color(r3c4) = color([r4c5=r7c3]). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r3c4=r4c5=r7c3], r3c7, [r4c7=r7c5], r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Diamond {r4c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r4c3, r7c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r4c3).
      → color(r4c4) = color(r7c3). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c4=r7c3], r4c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r4c4=r7c3]).
      → color(r3c4) = color(r4c3). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], [r3c4=r4c3], [r4c4=r7c3], r4c7} (spine [r3c4=r4c3]—[r4c4=r7c3]).
      → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color(r4c7). Identify.
  5.  Diamond {[r3c4=r4c3], [r1c4=r2c3=r4c7], [r4c4=r7c3], r7c7} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r4c7]—[r4c4=r7c3]).
      → color([r3c4=r4c3]) = color(r7c7). Identify.
  6.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c3=r4c7], [r3c4=r4c3=r7c7], [r4c4=r7c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r4c7]—[r3c4=r4c3=r7c7]).
      → color(r2c7) = color([r4c4=r7c3]). Identify.
  7.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r4c4=r7c3], [r3c4=r4c3=r7c7], r3c8, r7c8}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 699/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=5 diamonds=5 branches=1 complete=true
110100000001000000000100100000100000001010100001010100000000000000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r5c3, r6c5:
      Case A: color(r5c3) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r4c4, [r5c3=r6c5]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r4c4).
            → color(r3c4) = color([r5c3=r6c5]). Identify.
        4.  K₄ on {[r3c4=r5c3=r6c5], r3c7, r5c7, r6c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r5c3) ≠ color(r6c5). Add edge.
        5.  Diamond {r5c7, r5c3, r5c5, r6c5} (spine r5c3—r5c5).
            → color(r5c7) = color(r6c5). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r5c5, r5c3, [r5c7=r6c5], r6c3} (spine r5c3—[r5c7=r6c5]).
            → color(r5c5) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        7.  Diamond {r3c4, [r1c4=r2c3], r4c4, [r5c5=r6c3]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r4c4).
            → color(r3c4) = color([r5c5=r6c3]). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r3c4=r5c5=r6c3], r3c7, [r5c7=r6c5], r6c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  3.  Diamond {r4c4, [r1c4=r2c3=r3c7], r4c7, r7c7} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r3c7]—r4c7).
      → color(r4c4) = color(r7c7). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r4c7, [r1c4=r2c3=r3c7], [r4c4=r7c7], r7c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3=r3c7]—[r4c4=r7c7]).
      → color(r4c7) = color(r7c3). Identify.
  5.  K₄ on {[r4c4=r7c7], [r4c7=r7c3], r4c8, r7c8}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r4c5, r7c6:
      Case A: color(r4c5) = color(r7c6). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {[r1c4=r2c3], r3c5, r3c6, [r4c5=r7c6]} (spine r3c5—r3c6).
            → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color([r4c5=r7c6]). Identify.
        4.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c3=r4c5=r7c6], r2c7, r4c7, r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r4c5) ≠ color(r7c6). Add edge.
        5.  Diamond {r4c7, r4c5, r4c6, r7c6} (spine r4c5—r4c6).
            → color(r4c7) = color(r7c6). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r4c6, r4c5, [r4c7=r7c6], r7c5} (spine r4c5—[r4c7=r7c6]).
            → color(r4c6) = color(r7c5). Identify.

            → color([r1c4=r2c3]) = color([r4c6=r7c5]). Identify.
        8.  K₄ on {[r1c4=r2c3=r4c6=r7c5], r2c7, [r4c7=r7c6], r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

  2.  Diamond {r4c7, r8c7, r9c7, r7c8} (spine r8c7—r9c7).
      → color(r4c7) = color(r7c8). Identify.
  3.  Diamond {r4c4, r4c5, [r4c7=r7c8], r7c5} (spine r4c5—[r4c7=r7c8]).
      → color(r4c4) = color(r7c5). Identify.
  4.  Diamond {r3c5, [r1c4=r2c3], [r4c4=r7c5], r7c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—[r4c4=r7c5]).
      → color(r3c5) = color(r7c3). Identify.
  5.  K₄ on {[r3c5=r7c3], [r4c4=r7c5], r4c5, [r4c7=r7c8]}. Contradiction.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

            → color(r4c8) = color(r7c4). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r2c7, [r1c4=r2c3], r2c8, [r4c8=r7c4]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r2c8).
            → color(r2c7) = color([r4c8=r7c4]). Identify.
        7.  K₄ on {[r2c7=r4c8=r7c4], r8c5, r8c7, r8c8}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

pattern 765/832: PROVED cells=13 depth=4 diamonds=4 branches=1 complete=true
110100000001000000000000000000100000001010100001010100000100100000000000000000000
Proof of non-3-colorability:
  Assume for contradiction it is 3-colorable.

  1.  Diamond {r1c4, r1c1, r1c2, r2c3} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
      → color(r1c4) = color(r2c3). Identify.
  2.  Branch on r5c5, r7c4:
      Case A: color(r5c5) = color(r7c4). Identify.
        3.  Diamond {[r5c5=r7c4], [r1c4=r2c3], r5c3, r6c3} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r5c3).
            → color([r5c5=r7c4]) = color(r6c3). Identify.
        4.  K₄ on {[r5c5=r6c3=r7c4], r5c7, r6c7, r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r5c5) ≠ color(r7c4). Add edge.
        5.  Diamond {r6c5, r4c4, r5c5, r7c4} (spine r4c4—r5c5).
            → color(r6c5) = color(r7c4). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {r5c3, [r1c4=r2c3], r6c3, [r6c5=r7c4]} (spine [r1c4=r2c3]—r6c3).
            → color(r5c3) = color([r6c5=r7c4]). Identify.
        7.  K₄ on {[r5c3=r6c5=r7c4], r5c7, r6c7, r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □

        5.  Diamond {[r2c3=r4c1], [r1c1=r2c7], [r1c2=r2c4=r7c1], r7c7} (spine [r1c1=r2c7]—[r1c2=r2c4=r7c1]).
            → color([r2c3=r4c1]) = color(r7c7). Identify.
        6.  Diamond {[r1c2=r2c4=r7c1], [r1c1=r2c7], [r2c3=r4c1=r7c7], r6c7} (spine [r1c1=r2c7]—[r2c3=r4c1=r7c7]).
            → color([r1c2=r2c4=r7c1]) = color(r6c7). Identify.
        7.  K₄ on {[r1c2=r2c4=r6c7=r7c1], [r2c3=r4c1=r7c7], r5c2, r6c3}. Contradiction.
      Case B: color(r2c4) ≠ color(r7c1). Add edge.
        8.  Diamond {r6c4, r2c4, r7c4, r7c1} (spine r2c4—r7c4).
            → color(r6c4) = color(r7c1). Identify.
        9.  Diamond {r5c2, r4c1, r6c3, [r6c4=r7c1]} (spine r4c1—r6c3).
            → color(r5c2) = color([r6c4=r7c1]). Identify.
        10.  Diamond {r2c3, r1c1, r1c2, [r5c2=r6c4=r7c1]} (spine r1c1—r1c2).
            → color(r2c3) = color([r5c2=r6c4=r7c1]). Identify.
        11.  K₄ on {[r2c3=r5c2=r6c4=r7c1], r2c7, r6c7, r7c7}. Contradiction.
      Both cases contradict 3-colorability.

  Therefore the pattern is not 3-colorable. □
